<div class="main_contit">
            <h2>实验室主任介绍</h2>
            <p>作者：    时间：2019-03-19    点击数：<script>_showDynClicks("wbnews", 1449243745, 1071)</script></p>
        </div>
    <div class="main_conDiv" id="vsb_content"><p style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 21pt; font-family: 宋体;">孙立贤</span><span style="color: rgb(12, 82, 83); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 12pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">教授</span> (sunlx@guet.edu.cn)</span><span style="color: rgb(12, 82, 83); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;">&nbsp;</span><a href="javascript:leaveMessageConfirm()"><span style="color: rgb(51, 153, 153); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></a><a href="javascript:leaveMessageConfirm()"><span style="color: rgb(155, 59, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; text-decoration: underline;">&nbsp;</span></a></p>
<p style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;"><span style="color: rgb(12, 82, 83); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">桂林电子科技大学</span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 11.25pt;"><span style="color: rgb(12, 82, 83); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">研究领域：新能源（储氢、制氢、相变储能）材料、（生物）燃料电池、镍氢</span>/<span style="font-family: 宋体;">锂离子电池、新型催化剂、热化学、传感器、二氧化碳捕获、煤</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">重油洁净燃烧、建筑节能</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 等线; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt;"> </span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 22.5pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(34, 153, 153); font-size: 13.5pt; font-family: 宋体;">个人简介</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">分别于</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">1984</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">年、</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">1987</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">年、</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">1994</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">年在湖南大学分析化学专业获得理学学士、硕士、博士学位</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">(</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">师从俞汝勤院士</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">)</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">。</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">1995.2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">至</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">1995.4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">在日本通商产业省工业技术院研究员（获日本科技厅</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">STA fellowship </span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">资助</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">)</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">，</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">1995.5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">至</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">1996.10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">在德国耶拿大学化学系任德国洪堡基金研究人员，</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">1996.10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">至</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2001.8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">在日本产业技术综合研究所任特别研究员</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">(</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">获</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">AIST fellow</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">资助</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">)/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">产业技术研究员</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">(</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">获</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">NEDO fellowship </span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">资助</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">)</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">，</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2001.8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">至</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2012.11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">在中国科学院大连化学物理研究所任课题组长</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">研究员</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">博士生导师，任辽宁省能源材料热化学重点实验室主任。</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2012.12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">至今桂林电子科技大学教授</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">博士生导师，现任广西电子信息材料构效关系重点实验室主任。</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;">&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 宋体;">兼任国际化学热力学协会</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">(IACT)</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">理事与顾问，国际期刊《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Journal of Thermal Analysis </span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">＆ </span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Calorimetry</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》地区编辑，国际期刊《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">The Journal of Chemical Thermodynamics</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》编委，国际《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Inernational Journal of Electrochemistry Science</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》编委，国际《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Recent Patents on Corrosion Science</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》编委，中国化学会化学热力学与热分析专业委员会副主任，中国仪表功能材料学会储能与动力电池专业委员会委员，中国物理学会相图专业委员会委员。</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;">&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 宋体;">荣获中科院优秀</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">“</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">百人计划</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">人选，广西首批</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">八桂学者</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">，获国务院政府特殊津贴，英国皇家化学会会士，首届广西创新争先奖（</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">），</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2014~2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">年爱思唯尔</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">(Elsevier)</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">中国高被引学者，全国优秀科技工作者，大连市优秀专家称号，中科院优秀博士后合作导师，辽宁省第四批</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">“</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">百千万人才工程</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">百人层次人选，中国百篇最具影响国际学术论文，中国可再生能源学会氢能专业委员会优秀论文等。</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;">&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 宋体;">近年来主持国家</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">计划项目、</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">863</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">计划项目、国家自然科学基金重点项目、国家自然科学基金面上项目、国家自然基金联合项目、</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">IUPAC</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">国际合作项目、中国科学院知识创新工程重要方向项目、国家航天集团项目、广西重点实验室项目、广西协同创新中心项目、广西工程技术中心项目、广西人才小高地项目、广西自然科学基金项目、辽宁省科学技术基金项目、广东省</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">-</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">中科院联合基金项目、桂林市科技开发项目等</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">余项。</span></span><span style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt;">2018</span><span style="font-size: 10.5pt;">年承办诺贝尔奖获得者参加的石墨烯研究最新进展国际会议。</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;">&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 宋体;">出版学术著作《现代催化研究方法》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Classification of Materials, in Adaption of Simulated Annealing to Chemical Optimization Problems</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《物理化学学科前沿与展望》等</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">部；在《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Energy &amp; Environmental Science</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Journal of Materials Chemistry A</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Biosensors &amp; Bioelectronics</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Crystal Growth &amp; Design</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Journal of Physical Chemistry C</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Dalton Transactions</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">International Journal of Hydrogen Energy</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》等国内外重要学术刊物发表学术论文</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">330</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">余篇（其中</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">SCI</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">、</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">EI</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">收录</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">300</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">余篇）。</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;">&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 宋体;">开设本科生</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">研究生课程</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">门，指导硕士研究生</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">40</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">人、博士研究生</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">16</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">人。</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 等线; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt;"> </span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 22.5pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(34, 153, 153); font-size: 13.5pt; font-family: 宋体;">工作经历</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Georgia;">2012/12 - </span><span style="font-size: 10.5pt;">至今，桂林电子科技大学，材料科学与工程学院，教授，博士生导师</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Georgia;">2001/08 - 2012/11</span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt;">，中国科学院大连化学物理研究所，能源材料热化学重点实验室主任，组长，研究员，博士生导师</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Georgia;">1996/09 - 2001/08</span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt;">，日本产业技术综合研究所，特别研究员</span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Georgia;">/</span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt;">产业技术研究员</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Georgia;">1995/05 - 1996/09</span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt;">，德国耶拿大学化学系，德国洪堡基金研究人员</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Georgia;">1992/02 - 1995/01</span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt;">，湖南师范大学化学系，副教授</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 等线; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt;"> </span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 22.5pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(34, 153, 153); font-size: 13.5pt; font-family: 宋体;">主要荣誉</span></p>
<p style="text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">广西高等教育自治区级教学成果二等奖（2019）</span></p>

<p style="text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">辽宁省科技进步三等奖（2012）</span></p>
<p style="text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">广西首批”八桂学者”（2011~2016）</span></p>

<p><span style="color: rgb(34, 153, 153); font-size: 13.5pt;">学术活动</span><br></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">兼任国际化学热力学协会</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">(IACT)</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">理事与顾问，国际期刊《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Journal of Thermal Analysis </span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">＆ </span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Calorimetry</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》地区编辑，国际期刊《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">The Journal of Chemical Thermodynamics</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》编委，国际《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Inernational Journal of Electrochemistry Science</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》编委，国际《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Recent Patents on Corrosion Science</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》编委，中国化学会化学热力学与热分析专业委员会副主任，中国仪表功能材料学会储能与动力电池专业委员会委员，中国物理学会相图专业委员会委员，多次应邀担任国际国内学术会议大会共同主席，并作学术报告。</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;">&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 宋体;">荣获中科院优秀</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">“</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">百人计划</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">人选，获国务院政府特殊津贴，广西首批</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">八桂学者</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">，英国皇家化学会会士，首届广西创新争先奖（</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">），</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2014</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">至</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">年爱思唯尔中国高被引学者，大连市优秀专家称号，中科院优秀博士后合作导师，辽宁省第四批</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">“</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">百千万人才工程</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">百人层次人选，中国百篇最具影响国际学术论文，中国可再生能源学会氢能专业委员会优秀论文等。</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">近年来主持</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">IUPAC</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">国际合作项目、国家</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">计划项目、</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">863</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">计划项目、国家自然科学基金重点项目、国家自然科学基金面上项目、国家自然基金联合项目、中国科学院知识创新工程重要方向项目、国家航天集团项目、广西重点实验室项目、广西协同创新中心项目、广西工程技术中心项目、广西人才小高地项目、广西自然科学基金项目、辽宁省科学技术基金项目、广东省</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">-</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">中科院联合基金项目、桂林市科技开发项目等</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">余项；</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">出版学术著作《现代催化研究方法》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Classification of Materials, in Adaption of Simulated Annealing to Chemical Optimization Problems</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《物理化学学科前沿与展望》 《先进储氢材料导论》等</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">个章节；在《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Energy &amp; Environmental Science</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Journal of Materials Chemistry A</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Biosensors &amp; Bioelectronics</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Crystal Growth &amp; Design</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Journal of Physical Chemistry C</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Dalton Transactions</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">International Journal of Hydrogen Energy</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》等国内外重要学术刊物发表学术论文</span>400<span style="font-family: 宋体;">余篇（其中</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">SCI</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">、</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">EI</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">收录</span>400<span style="font-family: 宋体;">余篇）。</span></span><span style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt;">2018</span><span style="font-size: 10.5pt;">年主持诺贝奖获得者参加的石墨烯最新进展国际会议。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 等线; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt;"> </span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 22.5pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(34, 153, 153); font-size: 13.5pt; font-family: 宋体;">学术著作</span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;"></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: 宋体;">四个章节：</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: 宋体;">《现代催化研究方法》</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">《</span>Classification of Materials, in Adaption of Simulated Annealing to Chemical Optimization Problems<span style="font-family: 宋体;">》</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: 宋体;">《物理化学学科前沿与展望》</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: 宋体;">《先进储氢材料导论》</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 等线; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt;"> </span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 22.5pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(34, 153, 153); font-size: 13.5pt; font-family: 宋体;">科研项目</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 22.5pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(34, 153, 153); font-size: 13.5pt; font-family: 宋体;"></span></p>
<p style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px;"><span style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">[1]中德"电化学存储系统集成计算材料工程”联合实验室，中德合作课题，50万元，2019-2021，孙立贤</span></p>

<script language="javascript" src="../../_dwr/interface/NewsvoteDWR.js"></script><script language="javascript" src="../../_dwr/engine.js"></script><script language="javascript" src="/system/resource/js/news/newscontent.js"></script><script type="text/javascript">NewsvoteDWR.getNewsLinkUrl(1071,'1449243745','vsb',newsSkip);function newsSkip(data){if(data != ""){window.location.href = data;}}</script><script language="javascript" src="/system/resource/js/ajax.js"></script><form name="_newscontent_fromname">
<div class="main_content">
<div class="main_contit">
            <h2>实验室主任介绍</h2>
            <p>作者：    时间：2019-03-19    点击数：<script>_showDynClicks("wbnews", 1449243745, 1071)</script></p>
        </div>
    <div class="main_conDiv" id="vsb_content"><p style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 21pt; font-family: 宋体;">孙立贤</span><span style="color: rgb(12, 82, 83); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 12pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">教授</span> (sunlx@guet.edu.cn)</span><span style="color: rgb(12, 82, 83); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;">&nbsp;</span><a href="javascript:leaveMessageConfirm()"><span style="color: rgb(51, 153, 153); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></a><a href="javascript:leaveMessageConfirm()"><span style="color: rgb(155, 59, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; text-decoration: underline;">&nbsp;</span></a></p>
<p style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;"><span style="color: rgb(12, 82, 83); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">桂林电子科技大学</span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 11.25pt;"><span style="color: rgb(12, 82, 83); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">研究领域：新能源（储氢、制氢、相变储能）材料、（生物）燃料电池、镍氢</span>/<span style="font-family: 宋体;">锂离子电池、新型催化剂、热化学、传感器、二氧化碳捕获、煤</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">重油洁净燃烧、建筑节能</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 等线; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt;"> </span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 22.5pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(34, 153, 153); font-size: 13.5pt; font-family: 宋体;">个人简介</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">分别于</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">1984</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">年、</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">1987</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">年、</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">1994</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">年在湖南大学分析化学专业获得理学学士、硕士、博士学位</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">(</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">师从俞汝勤院士</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">)</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">。</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">1995.2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">至</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">1995.4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">在日本通商产业省工业技术院研究员（获日本科技厅</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">STA fellowship </span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">资助</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">)</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">，</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">1995.5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">至</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">1996.10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">在德国耶拿大学化学系任德国洪堡基金研究人员，</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">1996.10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">至</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2001.8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">在日本产业技术综合研究所任特别研究员</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">(</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">获</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">AIST fellow</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">资助</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">)/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">产业技术研究员</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">(</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">获</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">NEDO fellowship </span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">资助</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">)</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">，</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2001.8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">至</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2012.11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">在中国科学院大连化学物理研究所任课题组长</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">研究员</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">博士生导师，任辽宁省能源材料热化学重点实验室主任。</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2012.12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">至今桂林电子科技大学教授</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">博士生导师，现任广西电子信息材料构效关系重点实验室主任。</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;">&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 宋体;">兼任国际化学热力学协会</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">(IACT)</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">理事与顾问，国际期刊《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Journal of Thermal Analysis </span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">＆ </span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Calorimetry</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》地区编辑，国际期刊《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">The Journal of Chemical Thermodynamics</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》编委，国际《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Inernational Journal of Electrochemistry Science</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》编委，国际《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Recent Patents on Corrosion Science</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》编委，中国化学会化学热力学与热分析专业委员会副主任，中国仪表功能材料学会储能与动力电池专业委员会委员，中国物理学会相图专业委员会委员。</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;">&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 宋体;">荣获中科院优秀</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">“</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">百人计划</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">人选，广西首批</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">八桂学者</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">，获国务院政府特殊津贴，英国皇家化学会会士，首届广西创新争先奖（</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">），</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2014~2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">年爱思唯尔</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">(Elsevier)</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">中国高被引学者，全国优秀科技工作者，大连市优秀专家称号，中科院优秀博士后合作导师，辽宁省第四批</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">“</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">百千万人才工程</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">百人层次人选，中国百篇最具影响国际学术论文，中国可再生能源学会氢能专业委员会优秀论文等。</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;">&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 宋体;">近年来主持国家</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">计划项目、</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">863</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">计划项目、国家自然科学基金重点项目、国家自然科学基金面上项目、国家自然基金联合项目、</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">IUPAC</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">国际合作项目、中国科学院知识创新工程重要方向项目、国家航天集团项目、广西重点实验室项目、广西协同创新中心项目、广西工程技术中心项目、广西人才小高地项目、广西自然科学基金项目、辽宁省科学技术基金项目、广东省</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">-</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">中科院联合基金项目、桂林市科技开发项目等</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">余项。</span></span><span style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt;">2018</span><span style="font-size: 10.5pt;">年承办诺贝尔奖获得者参加的石墨烯研究最新进展国际会议。</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;">&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 宋体;">出版学术著作《现代催化研究方法》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Classification of Materials, in Adaption of Simulated Annealing to Chemical Optimization Problems</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《物理化学学科前沿与展望》等</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">部；在《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Energy &amp; Environmental Science</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Journal of Materials Chemistry A</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Biosensors &amp; Bioelectronics</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Crystal Growth &amp; Design</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Journal of Physical Chemistry C</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Dalton Transactions</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">International Journal of Hydrogen Energy</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》等国内外重要学术刊物发表学术论文</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">330</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">余篇（其中</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">SCI</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">、</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">EI</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">收录</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">300</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">余篇）。</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;">&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 宋体;">开设本科生</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">研究生课程</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">门，指导硕士研究生</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">40</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">人、博士研究生</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">16</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">人。</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 等线; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt;"> </span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 22.5pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(34, 153, 153); font-size: 13.5pt; font-family: 宋体;">工作经历</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Georgia;">2012/12 - </span><span style="font-size: 10.5pt;">至今，桂林电子科技大学，材料科学与工程学院，教授，博士生导师</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Georgia;">2001/08 - 2012/11</span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt;">，中国科学院大连化学物理研究所，能源材料热化学重点实验室主任，组长，研究员，博士生导师</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Georgia;">1996/09 - 2001/08</span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt;">，日本产业技术综合研究所，特别研究员</span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Georgia;">/</span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt;">产业技术研究员</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Georgia;">1995/05 - 1996/09</span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt;">，德国耶拿大学化学系，德国洪堡基金研究人员</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: Georgia;">1992/02 - 1995/01</span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 10.5pt;">，湖南师范大学化学系，副教授</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 等线; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt;"> </span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; line-height: 22.5pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><span style="color: rgb(34, 153, 153); font-size: 13.5pt; font-family: 宋体;">主要荣誉</span></p>

<p><span style="color: rgb(34, 153, 153); font-size: 13.5pt;">学术活动</span><br></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">兼任国际化学热力学协会</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">(IACT)</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">理事与顾问，国际期刊《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Journal of Thermal Analysis </span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">＆ </span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Calorimetry</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》地区编辑，国际期刊《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">The Journal of Chemical Thermodynamics</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》编委，国际《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Inernational Journal of Electrochemistry Science</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》编委，国际《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Recent Patents on Corrosion Science</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》编委，中国化学会化学热力学与热分析专业委员会副主任，中国仪表功能材料学会储能与动力电池专业委员会委员，中国物理学会相图专业委员会委员，多次应邀担任国际国内学术会议大会共同主席，并作学术报告。</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;">&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 宋体;">荣获中科院优秀</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">“</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">百人计划</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">人选，获国务院政府特殊津贴，广西首批</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">八桂学者</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">，英国皇家化学会会士，首届广西创新争先奖（</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">），</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2014</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">至</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">年爱思唯尔中国高被引学者，大连市优秀专家称号，中科院优秀博士后合作导师，辽宁省第四批</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">“</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">百千万人才工程</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">百人层次人选，中国百篇最具影响国际学术论文，中国可再生能源学会氢能专业委员会优秀论文等。</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">近年来主持</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">IUPAC</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">国际合作项目、国家</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">计划项目、</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">863</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">计划项目、国家自然科学基金重点项目、国家自然科学基金面上项目、国家自然基金联合项目、中国科学院知识创新工程重要方向项目、国家航天集团项目、广西重点实验室项目、广西协同创新中心项目、广西工程技术中心项目、广西人才小高地项目、广西自然科学基金项目、辽宁省科学技术基金项目、广东省</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">-</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">中科院联合基金项目、桂林市科技开发项目等</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">余项；</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left; text-indent: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt; mso-spacerun: &quot;yes&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;">出版学术著作《现代催化研究方法》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Classification of Materials, in Adaption of Simulated Annealing to Chemical Optimization Problems</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《物理化学学科前沿与展望》 《先进储氢材料导论》等</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">个章节；在《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Energy &amp; Environmental Science</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Journal of Materials Chemistry A</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Biosensors &amp; Bioelectronics</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Crystal Growth &amp; Design</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Journal of Physical Chemistry C</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">Dalton Transactions</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》《</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">International Journal of Hydrogen Energy</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">》等国内外重要学术刊物发表学术论文</span>400<span style="font-family: 宋体;">余篇（其中</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">SCI</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">、</span><span style="font-family: Georgia;">EI</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">收录</span>400<span style="font-family: 宋体;">余篇）。</span></span><span style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 10.5pt;">2018</span><span style="font-size: 10.5pt;">年主持诺贝奖获得者参加的石墨烯最新进展国际会议。</span></p>
